\DoxyCodeLine{1 \textcolor{comment}{/* stb\_image -\/ v2.14 -\/ public domain image loader -\/ http://nothings.org/stb\_image.h}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2 \textcolor{comment}{no warranty implied; use at your own risk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4 \textcolor{comment}{Do this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5 \textcolor{comment}{\#define STB\_IMAGE\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6 \textcolor{comment}{before you include this file in *one* C or C++ file to create the implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8 \textcolor{comment}{// i.e. it should look like this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{9 \textcolor{comment}{\#include ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{10 \textcolor{comment}{\#include ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{11 \textcolor{comment}{\#include ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{12 \textcolor{comment}{\#define STB\_IMAGE\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{13 \textcolor{comment}{\#include "{}stb\_image.h"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{14 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{15 \textcolor{comment}{You can \#define STBI\_ASSERT(x) before the \#include to avoid using assert.h.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{16 \textcolor{comment}{And \#define STBI\_MALLOC, STBI\_REALLOC, and STBI\_FREE to avoid using malloc,realloc,free}}
\DoxyCodeLine{17 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{18 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{19 \textcolor{comment}{QUICK NOTES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{20 \textcolor{comment}{Primarily of interest to game developers and other people who can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{21 \textcolor{comment}{avoid problematic images and only need the trivial interface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{22 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{23 \textcolor{comment}{JPEG baseline \& progressive (12 bpc/arithmetic not supported, same as stock IJG lib)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{24 \textcolor{comment}{PNG 1/2/4/8-\/bit-\/per-\/channel (16 bpc not supported)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{25 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{26 \textcolor{comment}{TGA (not sure what subset, if a subset)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{27 \textcolor{comment}{BMP non-\/1bpp, non-\/RLE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{28 \textcolor{comment}{PSD (composited view only, no extra channels, 8/16 bit-\/per-\/channel)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{29 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{30 \textcolor{comment}{GIF (*comp always reports as 4-\/channel)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{31 \textcolor{comment}{HDR (radiance rgbE format)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{32 \textcolor{comment}{PIC (Softimage PIC)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{33 \textcolor{comment}{PNM (PPM and PGM binary only)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{34 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{35 \textcolor{comment}{Animated GIF still needs a proper API, but here's one way to do it:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{36 \textcolor{comment}{http://gist.github.com/urraka/685d9a6340b26b830d49}}
\DoxyCodeLine{37 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{38 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ decode from memory or through FILE (define STBI\_NO\_STDIO to remove code)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{39 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ decode from arbitrary I/O callbacks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{40 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ SIMD acceleration on x86/x64 (SSE2) and ARM (NEON)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{41 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{42 \textcolor{comment}{Full documentation under "{}DOCUMENTATION"{} below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{43 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{44 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{45 \textcolor{comment}{Revision 2.00 release notes:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{46 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{47 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ Progressive JPEG is now supported.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{48 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{49 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ PPM and PGM binary formats are now supported, thanks to Ken Miller.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{50 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{51 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ x86 platforms now make use of SSE2 SIMD instructions for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{52 \textcolor{comment}{JPEG decoding, and ARM platforms can use NEON SIMD if requested.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{53 \textcolor{comment}{This work was done by Fabian "{}ryg"{} Giesen. SSE2 is used by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{54 \textcolor{comment}{default, but NEON must be enabled explicitly; see docs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{55 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{56 \textcolor{comment}{With other JPEG optimizations included in this version, we see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{57 \textcolor{comment}{2x speedup on a JPEG on an x86 machine, and a 1.5x speedup}}
\DoxyCodeLine{58 \textcolor{comment}{on a JPEG on an ARM machine, relative to previous versions of this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{59 \textcolor{comment}{library. The same results will not obtain for all JPGs and for all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{60 \textcolor{comment}{x86/ARM machines. (Note that progressive JPEGs are significantly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{61 \textcolor{comment}{slower to decode than regular JPEGs.) This doesn't mean that this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{62 \textcolor{comment}{is the fastest JPEG decoder in the land; rather, it brings it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{63 \textcolor{comment}{closer to parity with standard libraries. If you want the fastest}}
\DoxyCodeLine{64 \textcolor{comment}{decode, look elsewhere. (See "{}Philosophy"{} section of docs below.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{65 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{66 \textcolor{comment}{See final bullet items below for more info on SIMD.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{67 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{68 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ Added STBI\_MALLOC, STBI\_REALLOC, and STBI\_FREE macros for replacing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{69 \textcolor{comment}{the memory allocator. Unlike other STBI libraries, these macros don't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{70 \textcolor{comment}{support a context parameter, so if you need to pass a context in to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{71 \textcolor{comment}{the allocator, you'll have to store it in a global or a thread-\/local}}
\DoxyCodeLine{72 \textcolor{comment}{variable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{73 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{74 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ Split existing STBI\_NO\_HDR flag into two flags, STBI\_NO\_HDR and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{75 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_LINEAR.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{76 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_HDR:     suppress implementation of .hdr reader format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{77 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_LINEAR:  suppress high-\/dynamic-\/range light-\/linear float API}}
\DoxyCodeLine{78 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{79 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ You can suppress implementation of any of the decoders to reduce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{80 \textcolor{comment}{your code footprint by \#defining one or more of the following}}
\DoxyCodeLine{81 \textcolor{comment}{symbols before creating the implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{82 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{83 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{84 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{85 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_BMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{86 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{87 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_TGA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{88 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_GIF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{89 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_HDR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{90 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_PIC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{91 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_PNM   (.ppm and .pgm)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{92 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{93 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ You can request *only* certain decoders and suppress all other ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{94 \textcolor{comment}{(this will be more forward-\/compatible, as addition of new decoders}}
\DoxyCodeLine{95 \textcolor{comment}{doesn't require you to disable them explicitly):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{96 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{97 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_ONLY\_JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{98 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_ONLY\_PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{99 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_ONLY\_BMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{100 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_ONLY\_PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{101 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_ONLY\_TGA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{102 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_ONLY\_GIF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{103 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_ONLY\_HDR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{104 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_ONLY\_PIC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{105 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_ONLY\_PNM   (.ppm and .pgm)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{106 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{107 \textcolor{comment}{Note that you can define multiples of these, and you will get all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{108 \textcolor{comment}{of them ("{}only x"{} and "{}only y"{} is interpreted to mean "{}only x\&y"{}).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{109 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{110 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ If you use STBI\_NO\_PNG (or \_ONLY\_ without PNG), and you still}}
\DoxyCodeLine{111 \textcolor{comment}{want the zlib decoder to be available, \#define STBI\_SUPPORT\_ZLIB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{112 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{113 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ Compilation of all SIMD code can be suppressed with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{114 \textcolor{comment}{\#define STBI\_NO\_SIMD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{115 \textcolor{comment}{It should not be necessary to disable SIMD unless you have issues}}
\DoxyCodeLine{116 \textcolor{comment}{compiling (e.g. using an x86 compiler which doesn't support SSE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{117 \textcolor{comment}{intrinsics or that doesn't support the method used to detect}}
\DoxyCodeLine{118 \textcolor{comment}{SSE2 support at run-\/time), and even those can be reported as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{119 \textcolor{comment}{bugs so I can refine the built-\/in compile-\/time checking to be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{120 \textcolor{comment}{smarter.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{121 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{122 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ The old STBI\_SIMD system which allowed installing a user-\/defined}}
\DoxyCodeLine{123 \textcolor{comment}{IDCT etc. has been removed. If you need this, don't upgrade. My}}
\DoxyCodeLine{124 \textcolor{comment}{assumption is that almost nobody was doing this, and those who}}
\DoxyCodeLine{125 \textcolor{comment}{were will find the built-\/in SIMD more satisfactory anyway.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{126 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{127 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ RGB values computed for JPEG images are slightly different from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{128 \textcolor{comment}{previous versions of stb\_image. (This is due to using less}}
\DoxyCodeLine{129 \textcolor{comment}{integer precision in SIMD.) The C code has been adjusted so}}
\DoxyCodeLine{130 \textcolor{comment}{that the same RGB values will be computed regardless of whether}}
\DoxyCodeLine{131 \textcolor{comment}{SIMD support is available, so your app should always produce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{132 \textcolor{comment}{consistent results. But these results are slightly different from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{133 \textcolor{comment}{previous versions. (Specifically, about 3\% of available YCbCr values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{134 \textcolor{comment}{will compute different RGB results from pre-\/1.49 versions by +-\/1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{135 \textcolor{comment}{most of the deviating values are one smaller in the G channel.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{136 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{137 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ If you must produce consistent results with previous versions of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{138 \textcolor{comment}{stb\_image, \#define STBI\_JPEG\_OLD and you will get the same results}}
\DoxyCodeLine{139 \textcolor{comment}{you used to; however, you will not get the SIMD speedups for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{140 \textcolor{comment}{the YCbCr-\/to-\/RGB conversion step (although you should still see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{141 \textcolor{comment}{significant JPEG speedup from the other changes).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{142 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{143 \textcolor{comment}{Please note that STBI\_JPEG\_OLD is a temporary feature; it will be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{144 \textcolor{comment}{removed in future versions of the library. It is only intended for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{145 \textcolor{comment}{near-\/term back-\/compatibility use.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{146 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{147 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{148 \textcolor{comment}{Latest revision history:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{149 \textcolor{comment}{2.13  (2016-\/12-\/04) experimental 16-\/bit API, only for PNG so far; fixes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{150 \textcolor{comment}{2.12  (2016-\/04-\/02) fix typo in 2.11 PSD fix that caused crashes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{151 \textcolor{comment}{2.11  (2016-\/04-\/02) 16-\/bit PNGS; enable SSE2 in non-\/gcc x64}}
\DoxyCodeLine{152 \textcolor{comment}{RGB-\/format JPEG; remove white matting in PSD;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{153 \textcolor{comment}{allocate large structures on the stack;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{154 \textcolor{comment}{correct channel count for PNG \& BMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{155 \textcolor{comment}{2.10  (2016-\/01-\/22) avoid warning introduced in 2.09}}
\DoxyCodeLine{156 \textcolor{comment}{2.09  (2016-\/01-\/16) 16-\/bit TGA; comments in PNM files; STBI\_REALLOC\_SIZED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{157 \textcolor{comment}{2.08  (2015-\/09-\/13) fix to 2.07 cleanup, reading RGB PSD as RGBA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{158 \textcolor{comment}{2.07  (2015-\/09-\/13) partial animated GIF support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{159 \textcolor{comment}{limited 16-\/bit PSD support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{160 \textcolor{comment}{minor bugs, code cleanup, and compiler warnings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{161 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{162 \textcolor{comment}{See end of file for full revision history.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{163 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{209 \textcolor{comment}{// DOCUMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{210 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{211 \textcolor{comment}{// Limitations:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{212 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no 16-\/bit-\/per-\/channel PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{213 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no 12-\/bit-\/per-\/channel JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{214 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no JPEGs with arithmetic coding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{215 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no 1-\/bit BMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{216 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ GIF always returns *comp=4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{217 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{218 \textcolor{comment}{// Basic usage (see HDR discussion below for HDR usage):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{219 \textcolor{comment}{//    int x,y,n;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{220 \textcolor{comment}{//    unsigned char *data = stbi\_load(filename, \&x, \&y, \&n, 0);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{221 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... process data if not NULL ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{222 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... x = width, y = height, n = \# 8-\/bit components per pixel ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{223 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... replace '0' with '1'..'4' to force that many components per pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{224 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... but 'n' will always be the number that it would have been if you said 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{225 \textcolor{comment}{//    stbi\_image\_free(data)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{226 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{227 \textcolor{comment}{// Standard parameters:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{228 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *x                 -\/-\/ outputs image width in pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{229 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *y                 -\/-\/ outputs image height in pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{230 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *channels\_in\_file  -\/-\/ outputs \# of image components in image file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{231 \textcolor{comment}{//    int desired\_channels   -\/-\/ if non-\/zero, \# of image components requested in result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{232 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{233 \textcolor{comment}{// The return value from an image loader is an 'unsigned char *' which points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{234 \textcolor{comment}{// to the pixel data, or NULL on an allocation failure or if the image is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{235 \textcolor{comment}{// corrupt or invalid. The pixel data consists of *y scanlines of *x pixels,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{236 \textcolor{comment}{// with each pixel consisting of N interleaved 8-\/bit components; the first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{237 \textcolor{comment}{// pixel pointed to is top-\/left-\/most in the image. There is no padding between}}
\DoxyCodeLine{238 \textcolor{comment}{// image scanlines or between pixels, regardless of format. The number of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{239 \textcolor{comment}{// components N is 'req\_comp' if req\_comp is non-\/zero, or *comp otherwise.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{240 \textcolor{comment}{// If req\_comp is non-\/zero, *comp has the number of components that \_would\_}}
\DoxyCodeLine{241 \textcolor{comment}{// have been output otherwise. E.g. if you set req\_comp to 4, you will always}}
\DoxyCodeLine{242 \textcolor{comment}{// get RGBA output, but you can check *comp to see if it's trivially opaque}}
\DoxyCodeLine{243 \textcolor{comment}{// because e.g. there were only 3 channels in the source image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{244 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{245 \textcolor{comment}{// An output image with N components has the following components interleaved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{246 \textcolor{comment}{// in this order in each pixel:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{247 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{248 \textcolor{comment}{//     N=\#comp     components}}
\DoxyCodeLine{249 \textcolor{comment}{//       1           grey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{250 \textcolor{comment}{//       2           grey, alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{251 \textcolor{comment}{//       3           red, green, blue}}
\DoxyCodeLine{252 \textcolor{comment}{//       4           red, green, blue, alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{253 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{254 \textcolor{comment}{// If image loading fails for any reason, the return value will be NULL,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{255 \textcolor{comment}{// and *x, *y, *comp will be unchanged. The function stbi\_failure\_reason()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{256 \textcolor{comment}{// can be queried for an extremely brief, end-\/user unfriendly explanation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{257 \textcolor{comment}{// of why the load failed. Define STBI\_NO\_FAILURE\_STRINGS to avoid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{258 \textcolor{comment}{// compiling these strings at all, and STBI\_FAILURE\_USERMSG to get slightly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{259 \textcolor{comment}{// more user-\/friendly ones.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{260 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{261 \textcolor{comment}{// Paletted PNG, BMP, GIF, and PIC images are automatically depalettized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{262 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{263 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{264 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{265 \textcolor{comment}{// Philosophy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{266 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{267 \textcolor{comment}{// stb libraries are designed with the following priorities:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{268 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{269 \textcolor{comment}{//    1. easy to use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{270 \textcolor{comment}{//    2. easy to maintain}}
\DoxyCodeLine{271 \textcolor{comment}{//    3. good performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{272 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{273 \textcolor{comment}{// Sometimes I let "{}good performance"{} creep up in priority over "{}easy to maintain"{},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{274 \textcolor{comment}{// and for best performance I may provide less-\/easy-\/to-\/use APIs that give higher}}
\DoxyCodeLine{275 \textcolor{comment}{// performance, in addition to the easy to use ones. Nevertheless, it's important}}
\DoxyCodeLine{276 \textcolor{comment}{// to keep in mind that from the standpoint of you, a client of this library,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{277 \textcolor{comment}{// all you care about is \#1 and \#3, and stb libraries do not emphasize \#3 above all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{278 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{279 \textcolor{comment}{// Some secondary priorities arise directly from the first two, some of which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{280 \textcolor{comment}{// make more explicit reasons why performance can't be emphasized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{281 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{282 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Portable ("{}ease of use"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{283 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Small footprint ("{}easy to maintain"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{284 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ No dependencies ("{}ease of use"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{285 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{286 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{287 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{288 \textcolor{comment}{// I/O callbacks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{289 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{290 \textcolor{comment}{// I/O callbacks allow you to read from arbitrary sources, like packaged}}
\DoxyCodeLine{291 \textcolor{comment}{// files or some other source. Data read from callbacks are processed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{292 \textcolor{comment}{// through a small internal buffer (currently 128 bytes) to try to reduce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{293 \textcolor{comment}{// overhead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{294 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{295 \textcolor{comment}{// The three functions you must define are "{}read"{} (reads some bytes of data),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{296 \textcolor{comment}{// "{}skip"{} (skips some bytes of data), "{}eof"{} (reports if the stream is at the end).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{297 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{298 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{299 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{300 \textcolor{comment}{// SIMD support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{301 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{302 \textcolor{comment}{// The JPEG decoder will try to automatically use SIMD kernels on x86 when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{303 \textcolor{comment}{// supported by the compiler. For ARM Neon support, you must explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{304 \textcolor{comment}{// request it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{305 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{306 \textcolor{comment}{// (The old do-\/it-\/yourself SIMD API is no longer supported in the current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{307 \textcolor{comment}{// code.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{308 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{309 \textcolor{comment}{// On x86, SSE2 will automatically be used when available based on a run-\/time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{310 \textcolor{comment}{// test; if not, the generic C versions are used as a fall-\/back. On ARM targets,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{311 \textcolor{comment}{// the typical path is to have separate builds for NEON and non-\/NEON devices}}
\DoxyCodeLine{312 \textcolor{comment}{// (at least this is true for iOS and Android). Therefore, the NEON support is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{313 \textcolor{comment}{// toggled by a build flag: define STBI\_NEON to get NEON loops.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{314 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{315 \textcolor{comment}{// The output of the JPEG decoder is slightly different from versions where}}
\DoxyCodeLine{316 \textcolor{comment}{// SIMD support was introduced (that is, for versions before 1.49). The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{317 \textcolor{comment}{// difference is only +-\/1 in the 8-\/bit RGB channels, and only on a small}}
\DoxyCodeLine{318 \textcolor{comment}{// fraction of pixels. You can force the pre-\/1.49 behavior by defining}}
\DoxyCodeLine{319 \textcolor{comment}{// STBI\_JPEG\_OLD, but this will disable some of the SIMD decoding path}}
\DoxyCodeLine{320 \textcolor{comment}{// and hence cost some performance.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{321 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{322 \textcolor{comment}{// If for some reason you do not want to use any of SIMD code, or if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{323 \textcolor{comment}{// you have issues compiling it, you can disable it entirely by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{324 \textcolor{comment}{// defining STBI\_NO\_SIMD.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{325 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{326 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{327 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{328 \textcolor{comment}{// HDR image support   (disable by defining STBI\_NO\_HDR)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{329 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{330 \textcolor{comment}{// stb\_image now supports loading HDR images in general, and currently}}
\DoxyCodeLine{331 \textcolor{comment}{// the Radiance .HDR file format, although the support is provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{332 \textcolor{comment}{// generically. You can still load any file through the existing interface;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{333 \textcolor{comment}{// if you attempt to load an HDR file, it will be automatically remapped to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{334 \textcolor{comment}{// LDR, assuming gamma 2.2 and an arbitrary scale factor defaulting to 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{335 \textcolor{comment}{// both of these constants can be reconfigured through this interface:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{336 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{337 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_hdr\_to\_ldr\_gamma(2.2f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{338 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_hdr\_to\_ldr\_scale(1.0f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{339 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{340 \textcolor{comment}{// (note, do not use \_inverse\_ constants; stbi\_image will invert them}}
\DoxyCodeLine{341 \textcolor{comment}{// appropriately).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{342 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{343 \textcolor{comment}{// Additionally, there is a new, parallel interface for loading files as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{344 \textcolor{comment}{// (linear) floats to preserve the full dynamic range:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{345 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{346 \textcolor{comment}{//    float *data = stbi\_loadf(filename, \&x, \&y, \&n, 0);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{347 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{348 \textcolor{comment}{// If you load LDR images through this interface, those images will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{349 \textcolor{comment}{// be promoted to floating point values, run through the inverse of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{350 \textcolor{comment}{// constants corresponding to the above:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{351 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{352 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_ldr\_to\_hdr\_scale(1.0f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{353 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_ldr\_to\_hdr\_gamma(2.2f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{354 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{355 \textcolor{comment}{// Finally, given a filename (or an open file or memory block-\/-\/see header}}
\DoxyCodeLine{356 \textcolor{comment}{// file for details) containing image data, you can query for the "{}most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{357 \textcolor{comment}{// appropriate"{} interface to use (that is, whether the image is HDR or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{358 \textcolor{comment}{// not), using:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{359 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{360 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_is\_hdr(char *filename);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{361 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{362 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{363 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{364 \textcolor{comment}{// iPhone PNG support:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{365 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{366 \textcolor{comment}{// By default we convert iphone-\/formatted PNGs back to RGB, even though}}
\DoxyCodeLine{367 \textcolor{comment}{// they are internally encoded differently. You can disable this conversion}}
\DoxyCodeLine{368 \textcolor{comment}{// by by calling stbi\_convert\_iphone\_png\_to\_rgb(0), in which case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{369 \textcolor{comment}{// you will always just get the native iphone "{}format"{} through (which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{370 \textcolor{comment}{// is BGR stored in RGB).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{371 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{372 \textcolor{comment}{// Call stbi\_set\_unpremultiply\_on\_load(1) as well to force a divide per}}
\DoxyCodeLine{373 \textcolor{comment}{// pixel to remove any premultiplied alpha *only* if the image file explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{374 \textcolor{comment}{// says there's premultiplied data (currently only happens in iPhone images,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{375 \textcolor{comment}{// and only if iPhone convert-\/to-\/rgb processing is on).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{376 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{377 }
\DoxyCodeLine{378 }
\DoxyCodeLine{379 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STBI\_NO\_STDIO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{380 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#include <stdio.h>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{381 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif }\textcolor{comment}{// STBI\_NO\_STDIO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{382 }

\DoxyCodeLine{388 }

\DoxyCodeLine{390     \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55baf5829d16d4cca6077465c5abd346e2f8}{STBI\_grey\_alpha}} = 2,}

\DoxyCodeLine{667 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_NO\_SIMD}}

\DoxyCodeLine{670 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(\_\_MINGW32\_\_) \&\& defined(STBI\_\_X86\_TARGET) \&\& !defined(STBI\_MINGW\_ENABLE\_SSE2) \&\& !defined(STBI\_NO\_SIMD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{671 \textcolor{comment}{// Note that \_\_MINGW32\_\_ doesn't actually mean 32-\/bit, so we have to avoid STBI\_\_X64\_TARGET}}
\DoxyCodeLine{672 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{673 \textcolor{comment}{// 32-\/bit MinGW wants ESP to be 16-\/byte aligned, but this is not in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{674 \textcolor{comment}{// Windows ABI and VC++ as well as Windows DLLs don't maintain that invariant.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{675 \textcolor{comment}{// As a result, enabling SSE2 on 32-\/bit MinGW is dangerous when not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{676 \textcolor{comment}{// simultaneously enabling "{}-\/mstackrealign"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{677 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{678 \textcolor{comment}{// See https://github.com/nothings/stb/issues/81 for more information.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{679 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{680 \textcolor{comment}{// So default to no SSE2 on 32-\/bit MinGW. If you've read this far and added}}
\DoxyCodeLine{681 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/mstackrealign to your build settings, feel free to \#define STBI\_MINGW\_ENABLE\_SSE2.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{682 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_NO\_SIMD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{683 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}

\DoxyCodeLine{921 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{922     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} STBI\_MALLOC(size);}
\DoxyCodeLine{923 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{924 }
\DoxyCodeLine{925 \textcolor{comment}{// stb\_image uses ints pervasively, including for offset calculations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{926 \textcolor{comment}{// therefore the largest decoded image size we can support with the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{927 \textcolor{comment}{// current code, even on 64-\/bit targets, is INT\_MAX. this is not a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{928 \textcolor{comment}{// significant limitation for the intended use case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{929 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{930 \textcolor{comment}{// we do, however, need to make sure our size calculations don't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{931 \textcolor{comment}{// overflow. hence a few helper functions for size calculations that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{932 \textcolor{comment}{// multiply integers together, making sure that they're non-\/negative}}
\DoxyCodeLine{933 \textcolor{comment}{// and no overflow occurs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{934 }
\DoxyCodeLine{935 \textcolor{comment}{// return 1 if the sum is valid, 0 on overflow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{936 \textcolor{comment}{// negative terms are considered invalid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{937 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_addsizes\_valid(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b)}
\DoxyCodeLine{938 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{939     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b < 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{940     \textcolor{comment}{// now 0 <= b <= INT\_MAX, hence also}}
\DoxyCodeLine{941     \textcolor{comment}{// 0 <= INT\_MAX -\/ b <= INTMAX.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{942     \textcolor{comment}{// And "{}a + b <= INT\_MAX"{} (which might overflow) is the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{943     \textcolor{comment}{// same as a <= INT\_MAX -\/ b (no overflow)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{944     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} a <= INT\_MAX -\/ b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{945 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{946 }
\DoxyCodeLine{947 \textcolor{comment}{// returns 1 if the product is valid, 0 on overflow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{948 \textcolor{comment}{// negative factors are considered invalid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{949 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_mul2sizes\_valid(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b)}
\DoxyCodeLine{950 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{951     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (a < 0 || b < 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{952     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b == 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1; \textcolor{comment}{// mul-\/by-\/0 is always safe}}
\DoxyCodeLine{953                           \textcolor{comment}{// portable way to check for no overflows in a*b}}
\DoxyCodeLine{954     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} a <= INT\_MAX / b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{955 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{956 }
\DoxyCodeLine{957 \textcolor{comment}{// returns 1 if "{}a*b + add"{} has no negative terms/factors and doesn't overflow}}
\DoxyCodeLine{958 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_mad2sizes\_valid(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} add)}
\DoxyCodeLine{959 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{960     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_mul2sizes\_valid(a, b) \&\& stbi\_\_addsizes\_valid(a*b, add);}
\DoxyCodeLine{961 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{962 }
\DoxyCodeLine{963 \textcolor{comment}{// returns 1 if "{}a*b*c + add"{} has no negative terms/factors and doesn't overflow}}
\DoxyCodeLine{964 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_mad3sizes\_valid(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} add)}
\DoxyCodeLine{965 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{966     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_mul2sizes\_valid(a, b) \&\& stbi\_\_mul2sizes\_valid(a*b, c) \&\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{967         stbi\_\_addsizes\_valid(a*b*c, add);}
\DoxyCodeLine{968 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{969 }
\DoxyCodeLine{970 \textcolor{comment}{// returns 1 if "{}a*b*c*d + add"{} has no negative terms/factors and doesn't overflow}}
\DoxyCodeLine{971 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_mad4sizes\_valid(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} d, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} add)}
\DoxyCodeLine{972 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{973     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_mul2sizes\_valid(a, b) \&\& stbi\_\_mul2sizes\_valid(a*b, c) \&\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{974         stbi\_\_mul2sizes\_valid(a*b*c, d) \&\& stbi\_\_addsizes\_valid(a*b*c*d, add);}
\DoxyCodeLine{975 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{976 }
\DoxyCodeLine{977 \textcolor{comment}{// mallocs with size overflow checking}}
\DoxyCodeLine{978 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} *stbi\_\_malloc\_mad2(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} add)}
\DoxyCodeLine{979 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{980     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_mad2sizes\_valid(a, b, add)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} NULL;}

\DoxyCodeLine{982 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1694 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1695 \textcolor{comment}{//  "{}baseline"{} JPEG/JFIF decoder}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1696 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1697 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1698 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ doesn't support delayed output of y-\/dimension}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1699 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ simple interface (only one output format: 8-\/bit interleaved RGB)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1700 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ doesn't try to recover corrupt jpegs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1701 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ doesn't allow partial loading, loading multiple at once}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1702 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ still fast on x86 (copying globals into locals doesn't help x86)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1703 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ allocates lots of intermediate memory (full size of all components)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1704 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ non-\/interleaved case requires this anyway}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1705 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ allows good upsampling (see next)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1706 \textcolor{comment}{//    high-\/quality}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1707 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ upsampled channels are bilinearly interpolated, even across blocks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1708 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ quality integer IDCT derived from IJG's 'slow'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1709 \textcolor{comment}{//    performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1710 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ fast huffman; reasonable integer IDCT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1711 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ some SIMD kernels for common paths on targets with SSE2/NEON}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1712 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ uses a lot of intermediate memory, could cache poorly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1713 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1714 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STBI\_NO\_JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1715 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1716 \textcolor{comment}{// huffman decoding acceleration}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1717 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FAST\_BITS   9  }\textcolor{comment}{// larger handles more cases; smaller stomps less cache}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1718 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1719 \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1720 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1721     \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}}  fast[1 << FAST\_BITS];}

\DoxyCodeLine{1782 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_build\_huffman(stbi\_\_huffman *h, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *count)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1783 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1784     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, j, k = 0, code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1785     \textcolor{comment}{// build size list for each symbol (from JPEG spec)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1786     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < 16; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1787         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < count[i]; ++j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1788             h-\/>size[k++] = (\mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}})(i + 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1789     h-\/>size[k] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1790 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1791     \textcolor{comment}{// compute actual symbols (from jpeg spec)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1792     code = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1793     k = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1794     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 1; j <= 16; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1795         \textcolor{comment}{// compute delta to add to code to compute symbol id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1796         h-\/>delta[j] = k -\/ code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1797         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (h-\/>size[k] == j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1798             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (h-\/>size[k] == j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1799                 h-\/>code[k++] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(code++);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1800             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code -\/ 1 >= (1 << j)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad code lengths"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt JPEG"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{1801         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1802         \textcolor{comment}{// compute largest code + 1 for this size, preshifted as needed later}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1803         h-\/>maxcode[j] = code << (16 -\/ j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1804         code <<= 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1805     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1806     h-\/>maxcode[j] = 0xffffffff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1807 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1808     \textcolor{comment}{// build non-\/spec acceleration table; 255 is flag for not-\/accelerated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1809     memset(h-\/>fast, 255, 1 << FAST\_BITS);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1810     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < k; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1811         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} s = h-\/>size[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1812         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s <= FAST\_BITS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1813             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c = h-\/>code[i] << (FAST\_BITS -\/ s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1814             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} m = 1 << (FAST\_BITS -\/ s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1815             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < m; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1816                 h-\/>fast[c + j] = (\mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}})i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1817             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1818         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1819     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1820     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1821 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1822 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1823 \textcolor{comment}{// build a table that decodes both magnitude and value of small ACs in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1824 \textcolor{comment}{// one go.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1825 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_build\_fast\_ac(stbi\_\_int16 *fast\_ac, stbi\_\_huffman *h)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1826 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1827     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1828     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < (1 << FAST\_BITS); ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1829         \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} fast = h-\/>fast[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1830         fast\_ac[i] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1831         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (fast < 255) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1832             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} rs = h-\/>values[fast];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1833             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} run = (rs >> 4) \& 15;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1834             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} magbits = rs \& 15;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1835             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} len = h-\/>size[fast];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1836 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1837             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (magbits \&\& len + magbits <= FAST\_BITS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1838                 \textcolor{comment}{// magnitude code followed by receive\_extend code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1839                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} k = ((i << len) \& ((1 << FAST\_BITS) -\/ 1)) >> (FAST\_BITS -\/ magbits);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1840                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} m = 1 << (magbits -\/ 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1841                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k < m) k += (-\/1 << magbits) + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1842                 \textcolor{comment}{// if the result is small enough, we can fit it in fast\_ac table}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1843                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k >= -\/128 \&\& k <= 127)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1844                     fast\_ac[i] = (stbi\_\_int16)((k << 8) + (run << 4) + (len + magbits));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1845             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1846         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1847     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1848 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1849 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1850 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(stbi\_\_jpeg *j)}

\DoxyCodeLine{1852     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{1854         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b == 0xff) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{1870 \textcolor{comment}{// decode a jpeg huffman value from the bitstream}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1873     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1874     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c, k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1875 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1876     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j-\/>code\_bits < 16) stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1877 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1878     \textcolor{comment}{// look at the top FAST\_BITS and determine what symbol ID it is,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1879     \textcolor{comment}{// if the code is <= FAST\_BITS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1880     c = (j-\/>code\_buffer >> (32 -\/ FAST\_BITS)) \& ((1 << FAST\_BITS) -\/ 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1881     k = h-\/>fast[c];}

\DoxyCodeLine{1884         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s > j-\/>code\_bits)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1885             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}

\DoxyCodeLine{1887         j-\/>code\_bits -\/= s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1888         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} h-\/>values[k];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1889     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1890 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1891     \textcolor{comment}{// naive test is to shift the code\_buffer down so k bits are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1892     \textcolor{comment}{// valid, then test against maxcode. To speed this up, we've}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1893     \textcolor{comment}{// preshifted maxcode left so that it has (16-\/k) 0s at the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1894     \textcolor{comment}{// end; in other words, regardless of the number of bits, it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1895     \textcolor{comment}{// wants to be compared against something shifted to have 16;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1896     \textcolor{comment}{// that way we don't need to shift inside the loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1897     temp = j-\/>code\_buffer >> 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1898     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (k = FAST\_BITS + 1; ; ++k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1899         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (temp < h-\/>maxcode[k])}
\DoxyCodeLine{1900             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1901     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k == 17) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1902         \textcolor{comment}{// error! code not found}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1903         j-\/>code\_bits -\/= 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1904         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1905     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1906 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1907     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k > j-\/>code\_bits)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1908         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1909 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1910     \textcolor{comment}{// convert the huffman code to the symbol id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1911     c = ((j-\/>code\_buffer >> (32 -\/ k)) \& stbi\_\_bmask[k]) + h-\/>delta[k];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1912     STBI\_ASSERT((((j-\/>code\_buffer) >> (32 -\/ h-\/>size[c])) \& stbi\_\_bmask[h-\/>size[c]]) == h-\/>code[c]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1913 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1914     \textcolor{comment}{// convert the id to a symbol}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1915     j-\/>code\_bits -\/= k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1916     j-\/>code\_buffer <<= k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1917     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} h-\/>values[c];}

\DoxyCodeLine{2260                 \textcolor{comment}{// constants scaled things up by 1<<12; let's bring them back}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2272     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2273 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2274     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0, v = val, o = out; i < 8; ++i, v += 8, o += out\_stride) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2275         \textcolor{comment}{// no fast case since the first 1D IDCT spread components out}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2276         STBI\_\_IDCT\_1D(v[0], v[1], v[2], v[3], v[4], v[5], v[6], v[7])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2277             \textcolor{comment}{// constants scaled things up by 1<<12, plus we had 1<<2 from first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2278             \textcolor{comment}{// loop, plus horizontal and vertical each scale by sqrt(8) so together}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2279             \textcolor{comment}{// we've got an extra 1<<3, so 1<<17 total we need to remove.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2280             \textcolor{comment}{// so we want to round that, which means adding 0.5 * 1<<17,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2281             \textcolor{comment}{// aka 65536. Also, we'll end up with -\/128 to 127 that we want}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2282             \textcolor{comment}{// to encode as 0..255 by adding 128, so we'll add that before the shift}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2283             x0 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2284         x1 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2285         x2 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2286         x3 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2287         \textcolor{comment}{// tried computing the shifts into temps, or'ing the temps to see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2288         \textcolor{comment}{// if any were out of range, but that was slower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2289         o[0] = stbi\_\_clamp((x0 + t3) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2290         o[7] = stbi\_\_clamp((x0 -\/ t3) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2291         o[1] = stbi\_\_clamp((x1 + t2) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2292         o[6] = stbi\_\_clamp((x1 -\/ t2) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2293         o[2] = stbi\_\_clamp((x2 + t1) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2294         o[5] = stbi\_\_clamp((x2 -\/ t1) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2295         o[3] = stbi\_\_clamp((x3 + t0) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2296         o[4] = stbi\_\_clamp((x3 -\/ t0) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2297     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2298 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2299 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2729             STBI\_SIMD\_ALIGN(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}, data[64]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2730             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n = z-\/>order[0];}

\DoxyCodeLine{2736             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} h = (z-\/>img\_comp[n].y + 7) >> 3;}

\DoxyCodeLine{3255     \textcolor{comment}{// process groups of 8 pixels for as long as we can.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3257     \textcolor{comment}{// because we need to handle the filter boundary conditions.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3259 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(STBI\_SSE2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3260         \textcolor{comment}{// load and perform the vertical filtering pass}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3261         \textcolor{comment}{// this uses 3*x + y = 4*x + (y -\/ x)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3262         \_\_m128i zero = \_mm\_setzero\_si128();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3263         \_\_m128i farb = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) (in\_far + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3264         \_\_m128i nearb = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) (in\_near + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3265         \_\_m128i farw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(farb, zero);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3266         \_\_m128i nearw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(nearb, zero);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3267         \_\_m128i diff = \_mm\_sub\_epi16(farw, nearw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3268         \_\_m128i nears = \_mm\_slli\_epi16(nearw, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3269         \_\_m128i curr = \_mm\_add\_epi16(nears, diff); \textcolor{comment}{// current row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3270 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3271                                                    \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter works the same based on shifted vers of current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3272                                                    \textcolor{comment}{// row. "{}prev"{} is current row shifted right by 1 pixel; we need to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3273                                                    \textcolor{comment}{// insert the previous pixel value (from t1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3274                                                    \textcolor{comment}{// "{}next"{} is current row shifted left by 1 pixel, with first pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3275                                                    \textcolor{comment}{// of next block of 8 pixels added in.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3276         \_\_m128i prv0 = \_mm\_slli\_si128(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3277         \_\_m128i nxt0 = \_mm\_srli\_si128(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3278         \_\_m128i prev = \_mm\_insert\_epi16(prv0, t1, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3279         \_\_m128i next = \_mm\_insert\_epi16(nxt0, 3 * in\_near[i + 8] + in\_far[i + 8], 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3280 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3281         \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter, polyphase implementation since it's convenient:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3282         \textcolor{comment}{// even pixels = 3*cur + prev = cur*4 + (prev -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3283         \textcolor{comment}{// odd  pixels = 3*cur + next = cur*4 + (next -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3284         \textcolor{comment}{// note the shared term.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3285         \_\_m128i bias = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3286         \_\_m128i curs = \_mm\_slli\_epi16(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3287         \_\_m128i prvd = \_mm\_sub\_epi16(prev, curr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3288         \_\_m128i nxtd = \_mm\_sub\_epi16(next, curr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3289         \_\_m128i curb = \_mm\_add\_epi16(curs, bias);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3290         \_\_m128i even = \_mm\_add\_epi16(prvd, curb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3291         \_\_m128i odd = \_mm\_add\_epi16(nxtd, curb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3292 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3293         \textcolor{comment}{// interleave even and odd pixels, then undo scaling.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3294         \_\_m128i int0 = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16(even, odd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3295         \_\_m128i int1 = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16(even, odd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3296         \_\_m128i de0 = \_mm\_srli\_epi16(int0, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3297         \_\_m128i de1 = \_mm\_srli\_epi16(int1, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3298 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3299         \textcolor{comment}{// pack and write output}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3301         \_mm\_storeu\_si128((\_\_m128i *) (out + i * 2), outv);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3302 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#elif defined(STBI\_NEON)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3310 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3311                                                  \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter works the same based on shifted vers of current}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3317         int16x8\_t nxt0 = vextq\_s16(curr, curr, 1);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3319         int16x8\_t next = vsetq\_lane\_s16(3 * in\_near[i + 8] + in\_far[i + 8], nxt0, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3320 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3321         \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter, polyphase implementation since it's convenient:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3322         \textcolor{comment}{// even pixels = 3*cur + prev = cur*4 + (prev -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3323         \textcolor{comment}{// odd  pixels = 3*cur + next = cur*4 + (next -\/ cur)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3334         o.val[1] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(odd, 4);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3371 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef STBI\_JPEG\_OLD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3372 \textcolor{comment}{// this is the same YCbCr-\/to-\/RGB calculation that stb\_image has used}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3374 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define float2fixed(x)  ((int) ((x) * 65536 + 0.5))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3375 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_YCbCr\_to\_RGB\_row(\mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *out, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *pcb, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *pcr, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} step)}

\DoxyCodeLine{3378     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < count; ++i) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{3380         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r, g, b;}

\DoxyCodeLine{3382         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cb = pcb[i] -\/ 128;}

\DoxyCodeLine{3387         g >>= 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3388         b >>= 16;}

\DoxyCodeLine{3400 \textcolor{comment}{// this is a reduced-\/precision calculation of YCbCr-\/to-\/RGB introduced}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3402 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define float2fixed(x)  (((int) ((x) * 4096.0f + 0.5f)) << 8)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3403 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_YCbCr\_to\_RGB\_row(\mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *out, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *pcb, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *pcr, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} step)}

\DoxyCodeLine{3406     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < count; ++i) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{3435     \textcolor{comment}{// step == 3 is pretty ugly on the final interleave, and i'm not convinced}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3436     \textcolor{comment}{// it's useful in practice (you wouldn't use it for textures, for example).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3437     \textcolor{comment}{// so just accelerate step == 4 case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3438     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (step == 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3439         \textcolor{comment}{// this is a fairly straightforward implementation and not super-\/optimized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3440         \_\_m128i signflip = \_mm\_set1\_epi8(-\/0x80);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3444         \_\_m128i cb\_const1 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.77200f*4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3445         \_\_m128i y\_bias = \_mm\_set1\_epi8((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char})(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char})128);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3446         \_\_m128i xw = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(255); \textcolor{comment}{// alpha channel}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3448         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i + 7 < count; i += 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3449             \textcolor{comment}{// load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3450             \_\_m128i y\_bytes = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) (y + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3451             \_\_m128i cr\_bytes = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) (pcr + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3452             \_\_m128i cb\_bytes = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) (pcb + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3453             \_\_m128i cr\_biased = \_mm\_xor\_si128(cr\_bytes, signflip); \textcolor{comment}{// -\/128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3454             \_\_m128i cb\_biased = \_mm\_xor\_si128(cb\_bytes, signflip); \textcolor{comment}{// -\/128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3455 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3456                                                                    \textcolor{comment}{// unpack to short (and left-\/shift cr, cb by 8)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3457             \_\_m128i yw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(y\_bias, y\_bytes);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3458             \_\_m128i crw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), cr\_biased);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3459             \_\_m128i cbw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), cb\_biased);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3460 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3461             \textcolor{comment}{// color transform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3462             \_\_m128i yws = \_mm\_srli\_epi16(yw, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3463             \_\_m128i cr0 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(cr\_const0, crw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3464             \_\_m128i cb0 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(cb\_const0, cbw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3465             \_\_m128i cb1 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(cbw, cb\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3466             \_\_m128i cr1 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(crw, cr\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3467             \_\_m128i rws = \_mm\_add\_epi16(cr0, yws);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3468             \_\_m128i gwt = \_mm\_add\_epi16(cb0, yws);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3469             \_\_m128i bws = \_mm\_add\_epi16(yws, cb1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3470             \_\_m128i gws = \_mm\_add\_epi16(gwt, cr1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3471 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3472             \textcolor{comment}{// descale}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3473             \_\_m128i rw = \_mm\_srai\_epi16(rws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3474             \_\_m128i bw = \_mm\_srai\_epi16(bws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3475             \_\_m128i gw = \_mm\_srai\_epi16(gws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3476 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3477             \textcolor{comment}{// back to byte, set up for transpose}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3478             \_\_m128i brb = \_mm\_packus\_epi16(rw, bw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3479             \_\_m128i gxb = \_mm\_packus\_epi16(gw, xw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3480 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3481             \textcolor{comment}{// transpose to interleave channels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3482             \_\_m128i t0 = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(brb, gxb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3483             \_\_m128i t1 = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi8(brb, gxb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3484             \_\_m128i o0 = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16(t0, t1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3485             \_\_m128i o1 = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16(t0, t1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3486 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3487             \textcolor{comment}{// store}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3488             \_mm\_storeu\_si128((\_\_m128i *) (out + 0), o0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3489             \_mm\_storeu\_si128((\_\_m128i *) (out + 16), o1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3490             out += 32;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3491         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3492     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3493 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3494 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3495 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef STBI\_NEON}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3496     \textcolor{comment}{// in this version, step=3 support would be easy to add. but is there demand?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3497     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (step == 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3498         \textcolor{comment}{// this is a fairly straightforward implementation and not super-\/optimized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3499         uint8x8\_t signflip = vdup\_n\_u8(0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3500         int16x8\_t cr\_const0 = vdupq\_n\_s16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.40200f*4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3501         int16x8\_t cr\_const1 = vdupq\_n\_s16(-\/(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(0.71414f*4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3502         int16x8\_t cb\_const0 = vdupq\_n\_s16(-\/(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(0.34414f*4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3503         int16x8\_t cb\_const1 = vdupq\_n\_s16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.77200f*4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3504 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3505         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i + 7 < count; i += 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3506             \textcolor{comment}{// load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3507             uint8x8\_t y\_bytes = vld1\_u8(y + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3508             uint8x8\_t cr\_bytes = vld1\_u8(pcr + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3509             uint8x8\_t cb\_bytes = vld1\_u8(pcb + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3510             int8x8\_t cr\_biased = vreinterpret\_s8\_u8(vsub\_u8(cr\_bytes, signflip));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3511             int8x8\_t cb\_biased = vreinterpret\_s8\_u8(vsub\_u8(cb\_bytes, signflip));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3512 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3513             \textcolor{comment}{// expand to s16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3514             int16x8\_t yws = vreinterpretq\_s16\_u16(vshll\_n\_u8(y\_bytes, 4));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3515             int16x8\_t crw = vshll\_n\_s8(cr\_biased, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3516             int16x8\_t cbw = vshll\_n\_s8(cb\_biased, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3517 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3518             \textcolor{comment}{// color transform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3519             int16x8\_t cr0 = vqdmulhq\_s16(crw, cr\_const0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3520             int16x8\_t cb0 = vqdmulhq\_s16(cbw, cb\_const0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3521             int16x8\_t cr1 = vqdmulhq\_s16(crw, cr\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3522             int16x8\_t cb1 = vqdmulhq\_s16(cbw, cb\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3523             int16x8\_t rws = vaddq\_s16(yws, cr0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3524             int16x8\_t gws = vaddq\_s16(vaddq\_s16(yws, cb0), cr1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3525             int16x8\_t bws = vaddq\_s16(yws, cb1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3526 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3527             \textcolor{comment}{// undo scaling, round, convert to byte}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3528             uint8x8x4\_t o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3529             o.val[0] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(rws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3530             o.val[1] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(gws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3531             o.val[2] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(bws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3532             o.val[3] = vdup\_n\_u8(255);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3533 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3534             \textcolor{comment}{// store, interleaving r/g/b/a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3535             vst4\_u8(out, o);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3536             out += 8 * 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3537         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3538     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3539 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3540 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3541     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i < count; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3542         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y\_fixed = (y[i] << 20) + (1 << 19); \textcolor{comment}{// rounding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3543         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r, g, b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3544         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cr = pcr[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3545         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cb = pcb[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3546         r = y\_fixed + cr* float2fixed(1.40200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3547         g = y\_fixed + cr*-\/float2fixed(0.71414f) + ((cb*-\/float2fixed(0.34414f)) \& 0xffff0000);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3548         b = y\_fixed + cb* float2fixed(1.77200f);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3550         g >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3551         b >>= 20;}

\DoxyCodeLine{3554         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})b > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b < 0) b = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} b = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3555         out[0] = (\mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}})r;}

\DoxyCodeLine{3760 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3761 \textcolor{comment}{// public domain zlib decode    v0.2  Sean Barrett 2006-\/11-\/18}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3762 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3763 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ all input must be provided in an upfront buffer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3764 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ all output is written to a single output buffer (can malloc/realloc)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3765 \textcolor{comment}{//    performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3766 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ fast huffman}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3767 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3768 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STBI\_NO\_ZLIB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3769 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3770 \textcolor{comment}{// fast-\/way is faster to check than jpeg huffman, but slow way is slower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3771 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS  9 }\textcolor{comment}{// accelerate all cases in default tables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3772 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_ZFAST\_MASK  ((1 << STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS) -\/ 1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3773 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3774 \textcolor{comment}{// zlib-\/style huffman encoding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3775 \textcolor{comment}{// (jpegs packs from left, zlib from right, so can't share code)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3776 \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3777 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3778     stbi\_\_uint16 fast[1 << STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3779     stbi\_\_uint16 firstcode[16];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3780     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} maxcode[17];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3781     stbi\_\_uint16 firstsymbol[16];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3782     \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}}  size[288];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3783     stbi\_\_uint16 value[288];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3784 \} stbi\_\_zhuffman;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3785 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3786 stbi\_inline \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_bitreverse16(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3787 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3788     n = ((n \& 0xAAAA) >> 1) | ((n \& 0x5555) << 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3789     n = ((n \& 0xCCCC) >> 2) | ((n \& 0x3333) << 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3790     n = ((n \& 0xF0F0) >> 4) | ((n \& 0x0F0F) << 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3791     n = ((n \& 0xFF00) >> 8) | ((n \& 0x00FF) << 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3792     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} n;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3793 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3794 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3795 stbi\_inline \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_bit\_reverse(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} v, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} bits)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3796 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3797     STBI\_ASSERT(bits <= 16);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3798     \textcolor{comment}{// to bit reverse n bits, reverse 16 and shift}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3799     \textcolor{comment}{// e.g. 11 bits, bit reverse and shift away 5}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3800     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_bitreverse16(v) >> (16 -\/ bits);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3801 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3803 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_zbuild\_huffman(stbi\_\_zhuffman *z, \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *sizelist, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} num)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3804 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3805     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, k = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3806     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} code, next\_code[16], sizes[17];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3807 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3808     \textcolor{comment}{// DEFLATE spec for generating codes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3809     memset(sizes, 0, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(sizes));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3810     memset(z-\/>fast, 0, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(z-\/>fast));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3811     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < num; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3812         ++sizes[sizelist[i]];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3813     sizes[0] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3814     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 1; i < 16; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3815         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (sizes[i] >(1 << i))}
\DoxyCodeLine{3816             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad sizes"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt PNG"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{3817     code = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3818     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 1; i < 16; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3819         next\_code[i] = code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3820         z-\/>firstcode[i] = (stbi\_\_uint16)code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3821         z-\/>firstsymbol[i] = (stbi\_\_uint16)k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3822         code = (code + sizes[i]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3823         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (sizes[i])}
\DoxyCodeLine{3824             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code -\/ 1 >= (1 << i)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad codelengths"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt PNG"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{3825         z-\/>maxcode[i] = code << (16 -\/ i); \textcolor{comment}{// preshift for inner loop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3826         code <<= 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3827         k += sizes[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3828     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3829     z-\/>maxcode[16] = 0x10000; \textcolor{comment}{// sentinel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3830     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < num; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3831         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} s = sizelist[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3832         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3833             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c = next\_code[s] -\/ z-\/>firstcode[s] + z-\/>firstsymbol[s];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3834             stbi\_\_uint16 fastv = (stbi\_\_uint16)((s << 9) | i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3835             z-\/>size[c] = (\mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}})s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3836             z-\/>value[c] = (stbi\_\_uint16)i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3837             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s <= STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3838                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} j = stbi\_\_bit\_reverse(next\_code[s], s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3839                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (j < (1 << STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3840                     z-\/>fast[j] = fastv;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3841                     j += (1 << s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3842                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3843             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3844             ++next\_code[s];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3845         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3846     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3847     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3848 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3849 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3850 \textcolor{comment}{// zlib-\/from-\/memory implementation for PNG reading}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3851 \textcolor{comment}{//    because PNG allows splitting the zlib stream arbitrarily,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3852 \textcolor{comment}{//    and it's annoying structurally to have PNG call ZLIB call PNG,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3854 \textcolor{comment}{//    memory buffer}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3899     \textcolor{comment}{// use jpeg approach, which requires MSbits at top}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3900     k = stbi\_\_bit\_reverse(a-\/>code\_buffer, 16);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3905                             \textcolor{comment}{// code size is s, so:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3906     b = (k >> (16 -\/ s)) -\/ z-\/>firstcode[s] + z-\/>firstsymbol[s];}

\DoxyCodeLine{4230 \textcolor{comment}{// public domain "{}baseline"{} PNG decoder   v0.10  Sean Barrett 2006-\/11-\/18}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4231 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4232 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ only 8-\/bit samples}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4233 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ no CRC checking}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4234 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ allocates lots of intermediate memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4235 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ avoids problem of streaming data between subsystems}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4236 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ avoids explicit window management}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4237 \textcolor{comment}{//    performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4238 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ uses stb\_zlib, a PD zlib implementation with fast huffman decoding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4239 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4354             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_sub: cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}

\DoxyCodeLine{4361         \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4432     \textcolor{comment}{// we make a separate pass to expand bits to pixels; for performance,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4434     \textcolor{comment}{// intefere with filtering but will still be in the cache.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4435     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth < 8) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{4437             \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *cur = a-\/>out + stride*j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4438             \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *in = a-\/>out + stride*j + x*out\_n -\/ img\_width\_bytes;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4440             \textcolor{comment}{// png guarante byte alignment, if width is not multiple of 8/4/2 we'll decode dummy trailing data that will be skipped in the later loop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4441             \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} scale = (color == 0) ? stbi\_\_depth\_scale\_table[depth] : 1; \textcolor{comment}{// scale grayscale values to 0..255 range}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4442 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4443                                                                                \textcolor{comment}{// note that the final byte might overshoot and write more data than desired.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4444                                                                                \textcolor{comment}{// we can allocate enough data that this never writes out of memory, but it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4445                                                                                \textcolor{comment}{// could also overwrite the next scanline. can it overwrite non-\/empty data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4446                                                                                \textcolor{comment}{// on the next scanline? yes, consider 1-\/pixel-\/wide scanlines with 1-\/bit-\/per-\/pixel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4447                                                                                \textcolor{comment}{// so we need to explicitly clamp the final ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4448 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4449             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth == 4) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{4453                 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4455             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4456             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth == 2) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{4462                 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4465                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k > 2) *cur++ = scale * ((*in >> 2) \& 0x03);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4466             \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4472                     *cur++ = scale * ((*in >> 4) \& 0x01);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4473                     *cur++ = scale * ((*in >> 3) \& 0x01);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4474                     *cur++ = scale * ((*in >> 2) \& 0x01);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4475                     *cur++ = scale * ((*in >> 1) \& 0x01);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4476                     *cur++ = scale * ((*in) \& 0x01);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4477                 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4982 \textcolor{comment}{// returns 0..31 for the highest set bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4983 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_high\_bit(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} z)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4984 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4985     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4986     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z == 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4987     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z >= 0x10000) n += 16, z >>= 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4988     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z >= 0x00100) n += 8, z >>= 8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4989     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z >= 0x00010) n += 4, z >>= 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4990     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z >= 0x00004) n += 2, z >>= 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4991     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z >= 0x00002) n += 1, z >>= 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4992     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} n;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4995 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_bitcount(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a)}

\DoxyCodeLine{4997     a = (a \& 0x55555555) + ((a >> 1) \& 0x55555555); \textcolor{comment}{// max 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4998     a = (a \& 0x33333333) + ((a >> 2) \& 0x33333333); \textcolor{comment}{// max 4}}

\DoxyCodeLine{5000     a = (a + (a >> 8)); \textcolor{comment}{// max 16 per 8 bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5001     a = (a + (a >> 16)); \textcolor{comment}{// max 32 per 8 bits}}
