\DoxyCodeLine{5478             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} row = tga\_inverted ? tga\_height -\/ i -\/ 1 : i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5479             \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *tga\_row = tga\_data + row*tga\_width*tga\_comp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5480             stbi\_\_getn(s, tga\_row, tga\_width * tga\_comp);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5481         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5482     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5483     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5484         \textcolor{comment}{//   do I need to load a palette?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5485         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tga\_indexed)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5486         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5487             \textcolor{comment}{//   any data to skip? (offset usually = 0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5488             stbi\_\_skip(s, tga\_palette\_start);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5489             \textcolor{comment}{//   load the palette}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5490             tga\_palette = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)stbi\_\_malloc\_mad2(tga\_palette\_len, tga\_comp, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5491             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!tga\_palette) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5492                 STBI\_FREE(tga\_data);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5493                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}outofmem"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Out of memory"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5494             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5495             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tga\_rgb16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5496                 \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *pal\_entry = tga\_palette;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5497                 STBI\_ASSERT(tga\_comp == \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55baa59123e5d0af25f9b1539f5cf1facddf}{STBI\_rgb}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5498                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < tga\_palette\_len; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5499                     stbi\_\_tga\_read\_rgb16(s, pal\_entry);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5500                     pal\_entry += tga\_comp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5501                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5502             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5503             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_getn(s, tga\_palette, tga\_palette\_len * tga\_comp)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5504                 STBI\_FREE(tga\_data);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5505                 STBI\_FREE(tga\_palette);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5506                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad palette"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt TGA"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5507             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5508         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5509         \textcolor{comment}{//   load the data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5510         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < tga\_width * tga\_height; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5511         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5512             \textcolor{comment}{//   if I'm in RLE mode, do I need to get a RLE stbi\_\_pngchunk?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5513             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tga\_is\_RLE)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5514             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5515                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (RLE\_count == 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5516                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5517                     \textcolor{comment}{//   yep, get the next byte as a RLE command}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5518                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} RLE\_cmd = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5519                     RLE\_count = 1 + (RLE\_cmd \& 127);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5520                     RLE\_repeating = RLE\_cmd >> 7;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5521                     read\_next\_pixel = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5522                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5523                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!RLE\_repeating)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5524                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5525                     read\_next\_pixel = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5526                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5527             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5528             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5529             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5530                 read\_next\_pixel = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5531             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5532             \textcolor{comment}{//   OK, if I need to read a pixel, do it now}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5533             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (read\_next\_pixel)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5534             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5535                 \textcolor{comment}{//   load however much data we did have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5536                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tga\_indexed)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5537                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5538                     \textcolor{comment}{// read in index, then perform the lookup}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5539                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pal\_idx = (tga\_bits\_per\_pixel == 8) ? stbi\_\_get8(s) : stbi\_\_get16le(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5540                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pal\_idx >= tga\_palette\_len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5541                         \textcolor{comment}{// invalid index}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5542                         pal\_idx = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5543                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5544                     pal\_idx *= tga\_comp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5545                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < tga\_comp; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5546                         raw\_data[j] = tga\_palette[pal\_idx + j];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5547                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5548                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5549                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tga\_rgb16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5550                     STBI\_ASSERT(tga\_comp == \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55baa59123e5d0af25f9b1539f5cf1facddf}{STBI\_rgb}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5551                     stbi\_\_tga\_read\_rgb16(s, raw\_data);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5552                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5553                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5554                     \textcolor{comment}{//   read in the data raw}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5555                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < tga\_comp; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5556                         raw\_data[j] = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5557                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5558                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5559                 \textcolor{comment}{//   clear the reading flag for the next pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5560                 read\_next\_pixel = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5561             \} \textcolor{comment}{// end of reading a pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5562 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5563               \textcolor{comment}{// copy data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5564             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < tga\_comp; ++j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5565                 tga\_data[i*tga\_comp + j] = raw\_data[j];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5566 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5567             \textcolor{comment}{//   in case we're in RLE mode, keep counting down}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5568             -\/-\/RLE\_count;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5569         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5570         \textcolor{comment}{//   do I need to invert the image?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5571         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tga\_inverted)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5572         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5573             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j * 2 < tga\_height; ++j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5574             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5575                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} index1 = j * tga\_width * tga\_comp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5576                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} index2 = (tga\_height -\/ 1 -\/ j) * tga\_width * tga\_comp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5577                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = tga\_width * tga\_comp; i > 0; -\/-\/i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5578                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5579                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} temp = tga\_data[index1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5580                     tga\_data[index1] = tga\_data[index2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5581                     tga\_data[index2] = temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5582                     ++index1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5583                     ++index2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5584                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5585             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5586         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5587         \textcolor{comment}{//   clear my palette, if I had one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5588         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tga\_palette != NULL)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5589         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5590             STBI\_FREE(tga\_palette);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5591         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5592     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5593 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5594     \textcolor{comment}{// swap RGB -\/ if the source data was RGB16, it already is in the right order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5595     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tga\_comp >= 3 \&\& !tga\_rgb16)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5596     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5597         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* tga\_pixel = tga\_data;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5598         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < tga\_width * tga\_height; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5599         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5600             \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} temp = tga\_pixel[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5601             tga\_pixel[0] = tga\_pixel[2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5602             tga\_pixel[2] = temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5603             tga\_pixel += tga\_comp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5604         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5605     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5606 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5607     \textcolor{comment}{// convert to target component count}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5608     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp \&\& req\_comp != tga\_comp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5609         tga\_data = stbi\_\_convert\_format(tga\_data, tga\_comp, req\_comp, tga\_width, tga\_height);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5610 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5611     \textcolor{comment}{//   the things I do to get rid of an error message, and yet keep}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5612     \textcolor{comment}{//   Microsoft's C compilers happy... [8\string^(}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5613     tga\_palette\_start = tga\_palette\_len = tga\_palette\_bits =}
\DoxyCodeLine{5614         tga\_x\_origin = tga\_y\_origin = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5615     \textcolor{comment}{//   OK, done}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5616     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} tga\_data;}

\DoxyCodeLine{5620 \textcolor{comment}{// *************************************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5621 \textcolor{comment}{// Photoshop PSD loader -\/-\/ PD by Thatcher Ulrich, integration by Nicolas Schulz, tweaked by STB}}

\DoxyCodeLine{5623 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STBI\_NO\_PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5624 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_psd\_test(stbi\_\_context *s)}

\DoxyCodeLine{5631 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_psd\_decode\_rle(stbi\_\_context *s, \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *p, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pixelCount)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5632 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5633     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, nleft, len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5634 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5635     count = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5636     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} ((nleft = pixelCount -\/ count) > 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5637         len = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5638         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len == 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5639             \textcolor{comment}{// No-\/op.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5640         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5641         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len < 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5642             \textcolor{comment}{// Copy next len+1 bytes literally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5643             len++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5644             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > nleft) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0; \textcolor{comment}{// corrupt data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5645             count += len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5646             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5647                 *p = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5648                 p += 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5649                 len-\/-\/;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5650             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5651         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5652         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5653             \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}}   val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5654             \textcolor{comment}{// Next -\/len+1 bytes in the dest are replicated from next source byte.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5655             \textcolor{comment}{// (Interpret len as a negative 8-\/bit int.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5656             len = 257 -\/ len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5657             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > nleft) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0; \textcolor{comment}{// corrupt data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5658             val = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5659             count += len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5660             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5661                 *p = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5662                 p += 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5663                 len-\/-\/;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5664             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5665         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5666     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5667 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5668     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5669 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5670 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5671 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} *stbi\_\_psd\_load(stbi\_\_context *s, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *x, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *y, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *comp, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} req\_comp, stbi\_\_result\_info *ri, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} bpc)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5672 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5673     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pixelCount;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5674     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} channelCount, compression;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5675     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} channel, i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5676     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} bitdepth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5677     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w, h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5678     \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5679     STBI\_NOTUSED(ri);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5680 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5681     \textcolor{comment}{// Check identifier}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5682     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbi\_\_get32be(s) != 0x38425053)   \textcolor{comment}{// "{}8BPS"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5683         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}not PSD"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt PSD image"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5684 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5685     \textcolor{comment}{// Check file type version.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5686     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbi\_\_get16be(s) != 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5687         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}wrong version"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Unsupported version of PSD image"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5688 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5689     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip 6 reserved bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5690     stbi\_\_skip(s, 6);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5691 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5692     \textcolor{comment}{// Read the number of channels (R, G, B, A, etc).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5693     channelCount = stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5694     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channelCount < 0 || channelCount > 16)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5695         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}wrong channel count"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Unsupported number of channels in PSD image"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5696 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5697     \textcolor{comment}{// Read the rows and columns of the image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5698     h = stbi\_\_get32be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5699     w = stbi\_\_get32be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5700 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5701     \textcolor{comment}{// Make sure the depth is 8 bits.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5702     bitdepth = stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5703     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bitdepth != 8 \&\& bitdepth != 16)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5704         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}unsupported bit depth"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD bit depth is not 8 or 16 bit"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5705 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5706     \textcolor{comment}{// Make sure the color mode is RGB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5707     \textcolor{comment}{// Valid options are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5708     \textcolor{comment}{//   0: Bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5709     \textcolor{comment}{//   1: Grayscale}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5710     \textcolor{comment}{//   2: Indexed color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5711     \textcolor{comment}{//   3: RGB color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5712     \textcolor{comment}{//   4: CMYK color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5713     \textcolor{comment}{//   7: Multichannel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5714     \textcolor{comment}{//   8: Duotone}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5715     \textcolor{comment}{//   9: Lab color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5716     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbi\_\_get16be(s) != 3)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5717         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}wrong color format"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD is not in RGB color format"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5718 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5719     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the Mode Data.  (It's the palette for indexed color; other info for other modes.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5720     stbi\_\_skip(s, stbi\_\_get32be(s));}
\DoxyCodeLine{5721 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5722     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the image resources.  (resolution, pen tool paths, etc)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5723     stbi\_\_skip(s, stbi\_\_get32be(s));}
\DoxyCodeLine{5724 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5725     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the reserved data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5726     stbi\_\_skip(s, stbi\_\_get32be(s));}
\DoxyCodeLine{5727 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5728     \textcolor{comment}{// Find out if the data is compressed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5729     \textcolor{comment}{// Known values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5730     \textcolor{comment}{//   0: no compression}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5731     \textcolor{comment}{//   1: RLE compressed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5732     compression = stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5733     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (compression > 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5734         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad compression"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD has an unknown compression format"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5735 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5736     \textcolor{comment}{// Check size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5737     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_mad3sizes\_valid(4, w, h, 0))}
\DoxyCodeLine{5738         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}too large"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt PSD"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5739 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5740     \textcolor{comment}{// Create the destination image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5741 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5742     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!compression \&\& bitdepth == 16 \&\& bpc == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5743         out = (\mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *)stbi\_\_malloc\_mad3(8, w, h, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5744         ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel = 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5745     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5746     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5747         out = (\mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *)stbi\_\_malloc(4 * w*h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5748 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5749     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!out) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}outofmem"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Out of memory"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5750     pixelCount = w*h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5751 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5752     \textcolor{comment}{// Initialize the data to zero.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5753     \textcolor{comment}{//memset( out, 0, pixelCount * 4 );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5754 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5755     \textcolor{comment}{// Finally, the image data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5756     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (compression) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5757         \textcolor{comment}{// RLE as used by .PSD and .TIFF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5758         \textcolor{comment}{// Loop until you get the number of unpacked bytes you are expecting:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5759         \textcolor{comment}{//     Read the next source byte into n.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5760         \textcolor{comment}{//     If n is between 0 and 127 inclusive, copy the next n+1 bytes literally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5761         \textcolor{comment}{//     Else if n is between -\/127 and -\/1 inclusive, copy the next byte -\/n+1 times.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5762         \textcolor{comment}{//     Else if n is 128, noop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5763         \textcolor{comment}{// Endloop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5764 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5765         \textcolor{comment}{// The RLE-\/compressed data is preceeded by a 2-\/byte data count for each row in the data,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5766         \textcolor{comment}{// which we're going to just skip.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5767         stbi\_\_skip(s, h * channelCount * 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5768 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5769         \textcolor{comment}{// Read the RLE data by channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5770         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (channel = 0; channel < 4; channel++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5771             \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5772 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5773             p = out + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5774             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channel >= channelCount) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5775                 \textcolor{comment}{// Fill this channel with default data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5776                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5777                     *p = (channel == 3 ? 255 : 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5778             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5779             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5780                 \textcolor{comment}{// Read the RLE data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5781                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_psd\_decode\_rle(s, p, pixelCount)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5782                     STBI\_FREE(out);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5783                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}corrupt"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad RLE data"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5784                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5785             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5786         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5787 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5788     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5789     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5790         \textcolor{comment}{// We're at the raw image data.  It's each channel in order (Red, Green, Blue, Alpha, ...)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5791         \textcolor{comment}{// where each channel consists of an 8-\/bit (or 16-\/bit) value for each pixel in the image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5792 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5793         \textcolor{comment}{// Read the data by channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5794         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (channel = 0; channel < 4; channel++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5795             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channel >= channelCount) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5796                 \textcolor{comment}{// Fill this channel with default data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5797                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bitdepth == 16 \&\& bpc == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5798                     stbi\_\_uint16 *q = ((stbi\_\_uint16 *)out) + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5799                     stbi\_\_uint16 val = channel == 3 ? 65535 : 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5800                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, q += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5801                         *q = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5802                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5803                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5804                     \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *p = out + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5805                     \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} val = channel == 3 ? 255 : 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5806                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5807                         *p = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5808                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5809             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5810             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5811                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel == 16) \{    \textcolor{comment}{// output bpc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5812                     stbi\_\_uint16 *q = ((stbi\_\_uint16 *)out) + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5813                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, q += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5814                         *q = (stbi\_\_uint16)stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5815                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5816                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5817                     \mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}} *p = out + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5818                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bitdepth == 16) \{  \textcolor{comment}{// input bpc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5819                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5820                             *p = (\mbox{\hyperlink{stb__image_8h_a28eb51a1512ce382ee50f20e1d04d50d}{stbi\_uc}})(stbi\_\_get16be(s) >> 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5821                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5822                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5823                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5824                             *p = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5825                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5826                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5827             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5828         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5829     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5830 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5831     \textcolor{comment}{// remove weird white matte from PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5832     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channelCount >= 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5833         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5834             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < w*h; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5835                 stbi\_\_uint16 *pixel = (stbi\_\_uint16 *)out + 4 * i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5836                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pixel[3] != 0 \&\& pixel[3] != 65535) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5837                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} a = pixel[3] / 65535.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5838                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} ra = 1.0f / a;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5839                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} inv\_a = 65535.0f * (1 -\/ ra);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5840                     pixel[0] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(pixel[0] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5841                     pixel[1] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(pixel[1] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5842                     pixel[2] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(pixel[2] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5843                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5844             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5845         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5846         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5847             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < w*h; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5848                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *pixel = out + 4 * i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5849                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pixel[3] != 0 \&\& pixel[3] != 255) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5850                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} a = pixel[3] / 255.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5851                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} ra = 1.0f / a;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5852                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} inv\_a = 255.0f * (1 -\/ ra);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5853                     pixel[0] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)(pixel[0] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5854                     pixel[1] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)(pixel[1] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5855                     pixel[2] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)(pixel[2] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5856                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5857             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5858         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5859     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5860 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5861     \textcolor{comment}{// convert to desired output format}}

\DoxyCodeLine{5865         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5866             out = stbi\_\_convert\_format(out, 4, req\_comp, w, h);}

\DoxyCodeLine{5868     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5869 }

\DoxyCodeLine{5871     *y = h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5872     *x = w;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5873 }
